[removeMemberUser(String, Long)](com/appiancorp/suiteapi/personalization/GroupService.html#removeMemberUser\(java.lang.String,java.lang.Long\)) - Method in interface com.appiancorp.suiteapi.personalization.[GroupService](com/appiancorp/suiteapi/personalization/GroupService.html "interface in com.appiancorp.suiteapi.personalization")

[Role.PermissionMergeStrategy](com/appiancorp/suiteapi/common/Role.PermissionMergeStrategy.html "interface in com.appiancorp.suiteapi.common") - Interface in [com.appiancorp.suiteapi.common](com/appiancorp/suiteapi/common/package-summary.html)

Takes a set of existing permissions and a set of new permissions and decides how to combine them into a result set.
